#Used to delete the database if one already exists - helps with re-running the SQL commands
DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS `LocalBank`;

#Creates the database, only if one doesn't already exist of the same name
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS `LocalBank`;

#Creates the customers table, with 11 atttributes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `Customers` (
  `CustomerID` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Title` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `FirstName` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `LastName` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `D.O.B` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `Address1` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `Address2` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `Address3` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `Address4` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PostCode` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MobilePhone` varchar(15) DEFAULT NULL UNIQUE,
  PRIMARY KEY (`CustomerID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

#Creates the account table, with 4 atttributes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `Account` (
  `AccountID` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `SortCode` int(6) NOT NULL,
  `AccountNumber` int(8) NOT NULL,
  `OpeningBalance` float(10, 2) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`AccountID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

#Creates the bank table, with 2 atttributes - making up the composite key
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `Bank` (
  `AccountID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (`AccountID`) REFERENCES Account(AccountID),
  FOREIGN KEY (`CustomerID`) REFERENCES Customers(CustomerID),
  UNIQUE (`AccountID`, `CustomerID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

#Creates the transactions table, with 4 atttributes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `Transactions` (
  `TransactionID` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `AccountID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `TransactionDate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `TransactionAmount` float(10, 2) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`TransactionID`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`AccountID`) REFERENCES Account(AccountID)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

#Creates the loans table, with 6 atttributes
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `Loans` (
  `LoanID` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `AccountID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `PaymentRate` float(10, 2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `NumberOfPayments` int(4) NOT NULL,
  `FirstPaymentDate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `MonthlyDueDate` int DEFAULT 1,
  PRIMARY KEY (`LoanID`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`AccountID`) REFERENCES Account(AccountID)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

Inserts all of the data/records into all of the Customer table attributes,
except for the Customer's CustomerID, since that is automatically generated 
with every record that is added. */
